NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE
GMAC FINANCIAL SERVICES INDIA LIMITED
Regd. Office: 117/1, Arihant E Park, II Floor, L B Road, Adyar, Chennai-600 020.
NOTICE

OF

WINDING UP

Notice is hereby given under Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, that the Members of the GMAC Financial
Services India Limited, in its Extraordinary General Meeting held on May 31, 2010 at its registered office have resolved
to wind up the affairs of the company as a members’ voluntary winding up.
(By Order of the Board)
For GMAC Financial Services India Limited,
Chennai,
21st June 2010.

V. VIJAYARAGHAVAN,
Director.
